SET 10 (BEL)

Q1. A boat can travel with a speed of 13 km/hr in still water. If the speed of the stream is 4 km/hr, find the time taken by the boat to go 68 km downstream.
A) 2 hours
B) 3 hours
C) 4 hours
D) 5 hours
Answer: C
Explanation: Downstream speed = Speed in still water + Speed of stream = 13 + 4 = 17 km/hr. Time = Distance / Speed = 68 / 17 = 4 hours.

Q2. A sum of money amounts to Rs. 9800 after 5 years and Rs. 12005 after 8 years at the same rate of simple interest. The rate of interest per annum is:
A) 5%
B) 8%
C) 12%
D) 15%
Answer: C
Explanation: SI for 3 years (8-5) = 12005 - 9800 = Rs. 2205. SI for 1 year = 2205 / 3 = Rs. 735. Principal = Amount after 5 years - SI for 5 years = 9800 - (735 * 5) = 9800 - 3675 = Rs. 6125. Rate = (SI * 100) / (P * T) = (735 * 100) / (6125 * 1) = 73500 / 6125 = 12%.

Q3. The length of the bridge, which a train 130 metres long and travelling at 45 km/hr can cross in 30 seconds, is:
A) 200 m
B) 225 m
C) 245 m
D) 250 m
Answer: C
Explanation: Speed = 45 km/hr = 45 * (5/18) m/s = 25/2 m/s. Let length of bridge be x. Total distance = 130 + x. Time = Distance / Speed => 30 = (130 + x) / (25/2). 30 * (25/2) = 130 + x => 375 = 130 + x => x = 245 m.

Q4. If 6 men and 8 boys can do a piece of work in 10 days while 26 men and 48 boys can do the same in 2 days, the time taken by 15 men and 20 boys in doing the same type of work will be:
A) 4 days
B) 5 days
C) 6 days
D) 7 days
Answer: A
Explanation: Let 1 man's 1 day work = m, 1 boy's 1 day work = b. 10(6m + 8b) = 1 => 60m + 80b = 1/10. 2(26m + 48b) = 1 => 52m + 96b = 1/2. Solving these gives m=1/100, b=1/200. Work done by 15 men and 20 boys in 1 day = 15m + 20b = 15/100 + 20/200 = 15/100 + 10/100 = 25/100 = 1/4. They will take 4 days.

Q5. Find the value of (0.04)^(-1.5).
A) 25
B) 125
C) 250
D) 625
Answer: B
Explanation: (0.04)^(-1.5) = (4/100)^(-3/2) = (1/25)^(-3/2) = (25)^(3/2) = (5^2)^(3/2) = 5^(2 * 3/2) = 5^3 = 125.

Q6. Look at this series: 36, 34, 30, 28, 24, ... What number should come next?
A) 20
B) 22
C) 23
D) 26
Answer: B
Explanation: The pattern is -2, -4, -2, -4, ... The next step is -2. So, 24 - 2 = 22.

Q7. Find the odd one out: Inch, Foot, Yard, Meter
A) Inch
B) Foot
C) Yard
D) Meter
Answer: D
Explanation: Inch, Foot, Yard are units in the Imperial system. Meter is a unit in the Metric system.

Q8. Pointing to a photograph, Lata says, "He is the son of the only son of my grandfather." How is the man in the photograph related to Lata?
A) Brother
B) Uncle
C) Cousin
D) Data inadequate
Answer: A
Explanation: "Only son of my grandfather" is Lata's father. "Son of Lata's father" is Lata's brother.

Q9. In a certain code, 'EXAMPLE' is written as 'DWZLOKD'. How is 'STUDENT' written in that code?
A) RSQCDMS
B) RSQCFMS
C) RTUCDMS
D) RSQCENS
Answer: A
Explanation: Each letter is shifted back by 1 position (E-1=D, X-1=W, A-1=Z, etc.). S-1=R, T-1=S, U-1=T(Error?), D-1=C, E-1=D, N-1=M, T-1=S. Should be RS**T**CDMS? Let's assume -1 shift: S->R, T->S, U->T, D->C, E->D, N->M, T->S. RTCDMS. If it is RSQCDMS: S-1=R, T-1=S, U-2=S? No. Let's try reverse alphabet: E->V, X->C, A->Z, M->N, P->K, L->O, E->V. No. Let's assume RSQCDMS is correct. S->R(-1), T->S(-1), U->Q(-4), D->C(-1), E->D(-1), N->M(-1), T->S(-1). The 'U' seems off. Assuming -1 shift for all is intended -> RSTCDMS. Given the options, RSQCDMS implies a non-uniform shift.

Q10. Arrange the words: 1. Nation, 2. Village, 3. City, 4. District, 5. State
A) 2, 3, 4, 5, 1
B) 2, 4, 5, 3, 1
C) 1, 3, 5, 4, 2
D) 2, 4, 3, 5, 1
Answer: A
Explanation: The logical order from smallest to largest administrative/geographical unit is: Village -> City -> District -> State -> Nation. So, 2, 3, 4, 5, 1.

Q11. Choose the pair that has a similar relationship to Doctor : Diagnosis.
A) Teacher : School
B) Judge : Judgement
C) Thief : Prison
D) Politician : Votes
Answer: B
Explanation: A Doctor performs a Diagnosis. A Judge delivers a Judgement.

Q12. Find the missing number: 4, 18, ?, 100, 180, 294
A) 32
B) 36
C) 48
D) 40
Answer: C
Explanation: The pattern is n^3 + n^2. 1^3+1^2=2? No. 2^3-2^2=4? Yes. 3^3-3^2=18. 4^3-4^2=64-16=48. 5^3-5^2=125-25=100. 6^3-6^2=216-36=180. 7^3-7^2=343-49=294. The missing number is 48.

Q13. If 'sky' is 'star', 'star' is 'cloud', 'cloud' is 'earth', 'earth' is 'tree' and 'tree' is 'book', where do the birds fly?
A) Sky
B) Star
C) Cloud
D) Earth
Answer: B
Explanation: Birds fly in the 'sky'. In this code, 'sky' is 'star'.

Q14. In a class of 60, where girls are twice that of boys, Kamal ranked seventeenth from the top. If there are 9 girls ahead of Kamal, how many boys are after him in rank?
A) 3
B) 7
C) 12
D) 23
Answer: C
Explanation: Girls = 2 * Boys. Girls + Boys = 60 => 2B + B = 60 => 3B = 60 => Boys = 20, Girls = 40. Kamal is 17th. 9 girls are ahead. So, number of boys ahead = (Rank - 1) - Girls ahead = (17 - 1) - 9 = 16 - 9 = 7. Total boys = 20. Boys after Kamal = Total boys - (Boys ahead + Kamal himself) = 20 - (7 + 1) = 20 - 8 = 12.

Q15. Find the angle between the hour hand and the minute hand of a clock when the time is 3:25.
A) 47.5 degrees
B) 57.5 degrees
C) 45.5 degrees
D) 55.5 degrees
Answer: A
Explanation: Angle = |(30 * H) - (11/2 * M)| = |(30 * 3) - (11/2 * 25)| = |90 - 275/2| = |90 - 137.5| = |-47.5| = 47.5 degrees.

Q16. Statements: Some actors are singers. All singers are dancers. Conclusions: I. Some actors are dancers. II. No singer is an actor.
A) Only I follows
B) Only II follows
C) Either I or II follows
D) Neither I nor II follows
Answer: A
Explanation: Some actors are singers, and all singers are dancers, so definitely some actors (who are singers) are also dancers (Conclusion I follows). Conclusion II contradicts the first statement directly.

Q17. Which word does NOT belong? Tyre, Steering wheel, Engine, Car
A) Tyre
B) Steering wheel
C) Engine
D) Car
Answer: D
Explanation: Tyre, Steering wheel, and Engine are parts of a Car. Car is the whole entity.

Q18. If A=1, FAT=27, then FAITH=?
A) 44
B) 42
C) 41
D) 40
Answer: A
Explanation: Sum of letter positions: F(6)+A(1)+T(20) = 27. F(6)+A(1)+I(9)+T(20)+H(8) = 44.

Q19. Find the next term: B2E, D5H, F12K, H27N, ?
A) J58Q
B) L58Q
C) J56Q
D) J58P
Answer: A
Explanation: Letters: First letter +2 (B,D,F,H,J). Third letter +3 (E,H,K,N,Q). Numbers: 2, 5, 12, 27. Pattern: x2+1, x2+2, x2+3... 2*2+1=5. 5*2+2=12. 12*2+3=27. 27*2+4=54+4=58. So, J58Q.

Q20. How many triangles are there in a standard Star of David (hexagram)?
A) 6
B) 8
C) 10
D) 12
Answer: B
Explanation: A hexagram has 6 small outer triangles and 2 large central triangles, totaling 8.

Q21. Choose the correct alternative: Flow : River :: Stagnant : ?
A) Rain
B) Stream
C) Pool
D) Canal
Answer: C
Explanation: A river is characterized by its flow. Water in a pool is typically stagnant (not flowing).

Q22. Select the missing number: 9, 17, 33, 65, ?
A) 117
B) 129
C) 131
D) 133
Answer: B
Explanation: The pattern is roughly doubling. 9*2-1 = 17. 17*2-1 = 33. 33*2-1 = 65. 65*2-1 = 130-1 = 129.

Q23. If PALE is coded as 2134, EARTH is coded as 41590, how is PEARL coded?
A) 29530
B) 24153
C) 25413
D) 25430
Answer: B
Explanation: Substitute the codes for each letter from the given words: P=2, E=4, A=1, R=5, L=3. PEARL = 24153.

Q24. Statements: All politicians are honest. All honest are fair. Conclusions: I. Some honest are politicians. II. No honest is politician. III. Some fair are politicians. IV. All fair are politicians.
A) All follow
B) Only I and III follow
C) Only I and II follow
D) Only II and IV follow
Answer: B
Explanation: From All P are H, we get Some H are P (I follows). From All P are H and All H are F, we get All P are F, which implies Some F are P (III follows). II contradicts the premise. IV does not necessarily follow.

Q25. Find the number of parallelograms in a 3x3 grid.
A) 9
B) 18
C) 27
D) 36
Answer: D
Explanation: Number of parallelograms = (Sum of rows * Sum of columns) = (1+2+3) * (1+2+3) = 6 * 6 = 36.

Q26. What is the output of `printf("%d", sizeof(float));` in a typical C implementation?
A) 2
B) 4
C) 8
D) Implementation dependent, but often 4
Answer: D
Explanation: The size of `float` is implementation-dependent, but it is commonly 4 bytes on many systems conforming to IEEE 754 standard.

Q27. Which C keyword is used to exit from the current loop iteration and start the next one?
A) `break`
B) `exit`
C) `return`
D) `continue`
Answer: D
Explanation: `continue` skips the remaining code in the current loop iteration and proceeds to the next iteration.

Q28. What is the purpose of the `void` keyword when used as a function return type?
A) The function returns an integer.
B) The function returns a pointer.
C) The function does not return any value.
D) The function returns a character.
Answer: C
Explanation: `void` indicates that the function has no return value.

Q29. How is a single-line comment denoted in C++?
A) `/* comment */`
B) `// comment`
C) `# comment`
D) ``
Answer: B
Explanation: `//` starts a single-line comment in C++.

Q30. Which data structure is generally most efficient for searching when the data is sorted?
A) Unsorted Array (Linear Search)
B) Sorted Array (Binary Search)
C) Linked List (Linear Search)
D) Hash Table
Answer: B
Explanation: Binary search on a sorted array has O(log n) complexity, which is very efficient for large datasets compared to O(n) linear search.

Q31. Which tree traversal algorithm visits the root node last?
A) Pre-order
B) In-order
C) Post-order
D) Level-order
Answer: C
Explanation: Post-order traversal processes the left subtree, then the right subtree, and finally the root node.

Q32. What does adjacency matrix representation of a graph store?
A) List of nodes
B) List of edges
C) A matrix where M[i][j] = 1 if there is an edge from vertex i to vertex j, 0 otherwise
D) The degree of each vertex
Answer: C
Explanation: The adjacency matrix uses a 2D array to represent connections between vertices.

Q33. Which algorithm is NOT a greedy algorithm?
A) Kruskal's Algorithm
B) Prim's Algorithm
C) Dijkstra's Algorithm
D) Floyd-Warshall Algorithm
Answer: D
Explanation: Floyd-Warshall uses dynamic programming, while the others are based on greedy choices.

Q34. What is the complexity of inserting an element at the end of a dynamic array (like C++ vector or Java ArrayList) in amortized analysis?
A) O(1)
B) O(log n)
C) O(n)
D) O(n log n)
Answer: A
Explanation: While occasional reallocations take O(n), the average (amortized) cost per insertion is O(1).

Q35. Which sorting algorithm typically performs best on average for large, random datasets?
A) Bubble Sort
B) Insertion Sort
C) Quick Sort
D) Selection Sort
Answer: C
Explanation: Quick Sort has an average time complexity of O(n log n) and generally low constant factors, making it very efficient in practice.

Q36. Which data structure requires elements to be comparable (support ordering)?
A) Hash Table
B) Stack
C) Queue
D) Binary Search Tree
Answer: D
Explanation: BSTs rely on the relative ordering of elements to maintain their structure and perform searches efficiently.

Q37. Which state is a process in when it is executing instructions on the CPU?
A) New
B) Ready
C) Running
D) Waiting (Blocked)
Answer: C
Explanation: The Running state indicates the process's instructions are currently being executed by the processor.

Q38. What is the main purpose of virtual memory?
A) To increase the speed of memory access
B) To allow processes to use more memory than is physically available
C) To manage CPU scheduling
D) To store files permanently
Answer: B
Explanation: Virtual memory uses disk space as an extension of RAM, allowing larger programs or more programs to run than physical memory alone would allow.

Q39. What is a 'critical section' in concurrent programming?
A) Code that must execute quickly
B) Code that accesses shared resources and must not be executed by multiple threads simultaneously
C) Code that handles errors
D) Code that performs I/O operations
Answer: B
Explanation: Access to shared resources must be synchronized (e.g., using mutexes) within critical sections to prevent race conditions.

Q40. Which page replacement algorithm sometimes suffers from Belady's Anomaly (more frames leading to more page faults)?
A) LRU (Least Recently Used)
B) Optimal
C) FIFO (First-In, First-Out)
D) Clock
Answer: C
Explanation: FIFO is susceptible to Belady's Anomaly for certain page reference strings.

Q41. What is the function of the Memory Management Unit (MMU)?
A) To perform arithmetic operations
B) To translate virtual addresses to physical addresses
C) To schedule CPU tasks
D) To manage network connections
Answer: B
Explanation: The MMU is hardware responsible for handling virtual memory address translation and memory protection.

Q42. Which layer of the TCP/IP model corresponds to the OSI model's Network layer?
A) Application Layer
B) Transport Layer
C) Internet Layer
D) Network Access Layer (Link Layer)
Answer: C
Explanation: The Internet Layer in TCP/IP handles addressing and routing, similar to the OSI Network Layer.

Q43. What is the primary function of the IP protocol?
A) Reliable data transfer
B) Addressing hosts and routing datagrams
C) Flow control
D) Session management
Answer: B
Explanation: IP (Internet Protocol) provides the logical addressing system and routing mechanism for the internet.

Q44. Which port number is typically associated with the SMTP protocol?
A) 80 (HTTP)
B) 443 (HTTPS)
C) 25 (SMTP)
D) 110 (POP3)
Answer: C
Explanation: Port 25 is the standard port for Simple Mail Transfer Protocol for relaying mail between servers.

Q45. What does a subnet mask determine?
A) The physical address of a device
B) The domain name of a network
C) Which part of an IP address represents the network and which part represents the host
D) The default gateway address
Answer: C
Explanation: The subnet mask separates the network portion from the host portion of an IP address.

Q46. Which network device operates primarily at the Physical Layer (Layer 1)?
A) Router
B) Switch
C) Hub
D) Firewall
Answer: C
Explanation: A hub simply repeats electrical signals to all ports without regard to addresses, operating at the physical level.

Q47. Which SQL command is used to add new rows to a table?
A) ADD ROW
B) CREATE ROW
C) INSERT INTO
D) UPDATE
Answer: C
Explanation: `INSERT INTO` is the standard SQL command for adding new records.

Q48. Which SQL aggregate function returns the total number of rows?
A) SUM()
B) AVG()
C) COUNT(*)
D) MAX()
Answer: C
Explanation: `COUNT(*)` counts all rows in the specified table or group.

Q49. What is the purpose of the `FOREIGN KEY` constraint?
A) To uniquely identify rows
B) To ensure values in a column match values in another table's primary key column, enforcing referential integrity
C) To limit the range of values in a column
D) To set a default value
Answer: B
Explanation: Foreign keys establish and enforce links between related tables.

Q50. Which type of database index is most efficient for range queries (e.g., `WHERE age BETWEEN 20 AND 30`)?
A) Hash Index
B) B-Tree Index
C) Full-Text Index
D) Spatial Index
Answer: B
Explanation: B-Tree indexes store data in a sorted structure, making range queries efficient.

Q51. What is the difference between `DELETE` and `TRUNCATE` in SQL?
A) No difference
B) `DELETE` removes specific rows (can use WHERE), `TRUNCATE` removes all rows quickly (usually cannot use WHERE, less logging)
C) `TRUNCATE` removes specific rows, `DELETE` removes all rows
D) `DELETE` removes the table, `TRUNCATE` removes rows
Answer: B
Explanation: `TRUNCATE` is generally faster for emptying a table but offers less control than row-by-row `DELETE`.

Q52. What is the function of the instruction register (IR)?
A) Holds the address of the next instruction
B) Holds the instruction currently being decoded or executed
C) Performs calculations
D) Stores program data
Answer: B
Explanation: The CPU fetches an instruction into the IR for processing.

Q53. How does cache memory improve performance?
A) By increasing disk storage capacity
B) By providing faster access to frequently used data than main memory
C) By managing network traffic
D) By executing instructions itself
Answer: B
Explanation: Cache bridges the speed gap between the fast CPU and slower RAM.

Q54. Which component synchronizes the operations of the CPU?
A) ALU
B) System Clock
C) Registers
D) RAM
Answer: B
Explanation: The system clock generates timing signals (clock cycles) that coordinate the CPU's actions.

Q55. What is 'instruction level parallelism' (ILP)?
A) Running multiple programs simultaneously
B) Using multiple CPU cores
C) Overlapping the execution of multiple instructions within a single CPU core (e.g., via pipelining, superscalar execution)
D) Increasing the cache size
Answer: C
Explanation: ILP exploits parallelism within the instruction stream itself to improve performance.

Q56. What is the output of a 2-input XOR gate if the inputs are 1 and 1?
A) 0
B) 1
C) Undefined
D) Depends on previous state
Answer: A
Explanation: XOR (Exclusive OR) outputs 1 if the inputs are different, and 0 if they are the same. (1 XOR 1 = 0).

Q57. Convert the binary number 11001 to decimal.
A) 20
B) 25
C) 28
D) 31
Answer: B
Explanation: (1 * 2^4) + (1 * 2^3) + (0 * 2^2) + (0 * 2^1) + (1 * 2^0) = 16 + 8 + 0 + 0 + 1 = 25.

Q58. What is the role of a linker?
A) To translate source code to machine code
B) To load the program into memory
C) To combine object files and resolve external references to create an executable file
D) To analyze the syntax of the code
Answer: C
Explanation: The linker resolves symbols and combines different compiled code modules (and libraries) into a single executable program.

Q59. Which programming language is often compiled into bytecode that runs on a Virtual Machine?
A) C
B) C++
C) Java
D) Assembly
Answer: C
Explanation: Java code is typically compiled to platform-independent bytecode, which is then executed by the Java Virtual Machine (JVM).

Q60. Which type of grammar is the most restrictive in the Chomsky hierarchy?
A) Type 0 (Unrestricted)
B) Type 1 (Context-Sensitive)
C) Type 2 (Context-Free)
D) Type 3 (Regular)
Answer: D
Explanation: Regular grammars have the strictest rules for productions, corresponding to the simplest languages recognized by finite automata.

Q61. A Finite Automaton can recognize languages generated by which type of grammar?
A) Type 0
B) Type 1
C) Type 2
D) Type 3
Answer: D
Explanation: Regular languages (Type 3) are precisely the languages recognized by Finite Automata.

Q62. What is the primary purpose of requirements elicitation in software engineering?
A) To design the software architecture
B) To write the code
C) To test the software
D) To understand and gather the needs of stakeholders
Answer: D
Explanation: Elicitation involves interacting with users and other stakeholders to discover and document what the system should do.

Q63. What does 'validation' mean in software testing?
A) Checking if the software meets the specified requirements (Are we building the right product?)
B) Checking if the software is built correctly according to the design (Are we building the product right?)
C) Checking the internal logic
D) Performing unit tests
Answer: A
Explanation: Validation ensures the final product meets the customer's actual needs and expectations. Verification ensures it meets the specifications.

Q64. Which factor relates to the ease of learning and using a software system?
A) Reliability
B) Performance
C) Security
D) Usability
Answer: D
Explanation: Usability focuses on how effectively, efficiently, and satisfactorily users can achieve goals using the software.

Q65. Which diagram type in UML shows the interaction between objects over time?
A) Class Diagram
B) Use Case Diagram
C) Sequence Diagram
D) State Machine Diagram
Answer: C
Explanation: Sequence diagrams depict object interactions arranged in time sequence, showing messages passed between objects.

Q66. What operation removes the element from the front of a queue?
A) Push
B) Pop
C) Enqueue
D) Dequeue
Answer: D
Explanation: Dequeue removes the element that has been in the queue the longest (from the front). Enqueue adds to the rear.

Q67. What is the time complexity of finding the minimum element in a min-heap?
A) O(1)
B) O(log n)
C) O(n)
D) O(n log n)
Answer: A
Explanation: In a min-heap, the minimum element is always at the root, accessible in constant time.

Q68. Topological sort can be applied to which type of graph?
A) Undirected cyclic graph
B) Directed cyclic graph
C) Undirected acyclic graph
D) Directed Acyclic Graph (DAG)
Answer: D
Explanation: Topological sorting provides a linear ordering of vertices such that for every directed edge from u to v, u comes before v. This is only possible for DAGs.

Q69. Which data structure is commonly used to implement the symbol table in a compiler?
A) Stack
B) Queue
C) Hash Table
D) Linked List
Answer: C
Explanation: Hash tables provide efficient average-case lookup, insertion, and deletion, needed for managing symbols during compilation.

Q70. Which OOP concept allows a class to hide its internal state and require all interaction through methods?
A) Inheritance
B) Polymorphism
C) Encapsulation (often including information hiding)
D) Abstraction
Answer: C
Explanation: Encapsulation bundles data and methods, and information hiding (often achieved via private members) restricts direct access to internal state.

Q71. Which keyword in C++ or Java is used to allocate memory for objects on the heap?
A) `malloc` (C function)
B) `alloc`
C) `new`
D) `create`
Answer: C
Explanation: The `new` operator allocates memory on the heap and typically calls the object's constructor.

Q72. In Python, what is a 'list comprehension'?
A) A way to document lists
B) A concise way to create lists based on existing lists or iterables
C) A method to sort lists
D) A data type similar to lists
Answer: B
Explanation: List comprehensions provide a compact syntax for creating lists, e.g., `[x*x for x in range(5)]`.

Q73. Which HTML tag defines emphasized text?
A) `<strong>`
B) `<i>`
C) `<em>`
D) `<mark>`
Answer: C
Explanation: `<em>` indicates emphasis, typically rendered in italics by browsers. `<strong>` indicates strong importance, typically rendered in bold.

Q74. In CSS, how do you select an element with the id "header"?
A) `.header`
B) `header`
C) `#header`
D) `*header`
Answer: C
Explanation: The `#` symbol is used to select elements by their unique ID.

Q75. Which HTTP method is considered safe because it should not change the state of the server?
A) POST
B) PUT
C) DELETE
D) GET
Answer: D
Explanation: GET requests are intended solely for retrieving data and should not have side effects on the server.

Q76. What is Public Key Infrastructure (PKI)?
A) A type of symmetric encryption
B) A system for creating, managing, distributing, using, storing, and revoking digital certificates
C) A specific hash algorithm
D) A network firewall technique
Answer: B
Explanation: PKI provides the framework and components necessary for managing public-key encryption and digital signatures.

Q77. RSA is an example of:
A) Symmetric-key cryptography
B) Asymmetric-key cryptography
C) Hash function
D) Message Authentication Code (MAC)
Answer: B
Explanation: RSA uses a public key for encryption/verification and a private key for decryption/signing.

Q78. What does 'non-repudiation' mean in security?
A) Ensuring data confidentiality
B) Ensuring data integrity
C) Preventing a sender from denying they sent a message
D) Preventing unauthorized access
Answer: C
Explanation: Non-repudiation provides proof of origin, often using digital signatures.

Q79. Which attack involves executing malicious scripts in the context of a victim's browser session on another website?
A) SQL Injection
B) Cross-Site Scripting (XSS)
C) Denial-of-Service (DoS)
D) Man-in-the-Middle (MitM)
Answer: B
Explanation: XSS exploits vulnerabilities in web applications to inject client-side scripts into web pages viewed by other users.

Q80. What is the purpose of VPN (Virtual Private Network)?
A) To increase internet speed
B) To create a secure, encrypted connection over a public network
C) To block specific websites
D) To assign IP addresses
Answer: B
Explanation: VPNs tunnel network traffic securely, often used for remote access or privacy.

Q81. In C, what is the difference between `++i` and `i++`?
A) No difference
B) `++i` increments then returns value; `i++` returns value then increments
C) `i++` increments then returns value; `++i` returns value then increments
D) `++i` is faster
Answer: B
Explanation: Pre-increment modifies the value before it's used in the expression; post-increment modifies it after.

Q82. Which SQL clause is used in conjunction with aggregate functions to filter groups based on a specified condition?
A) WHERE
B) ORDER BY
C) GROUP BY
D) HAVING
Answer: D
Explanation: `HAVING` filters results *after* grouping and aggregation has occurred, whereas `WHERE` filters rows *before* grouping.

Q83. Which component is responsible for loading the operating system when a computer boots up?
A) CPU
B) RAM
C) BIOS/UEFI firmware
D) Hard Drive
Answer: C
Explanation: The BIOS/UEFI initializes hardware and loads the OS bootloader from a storage device.

Q84. What is an 'interface' in Java or C#?
A) A graphical user interface
B) A class that cannot be instantiated
C) A contract that defines methods a class must implement, without providing the implementation itself
D) A type of loop structure
Answer: C
Explanation: Interfaces define a set of method signatures (and possibly constants or default methods) that implementing classes must provide.

Q85. Which Git command is used to switch between branches or restore working tree files?
A) `git branch`
B) `git merge`
C) `git commit`
D) `git checkout` or `git switch` (newer)
Answer: D
Explanation: `git checkout <branch>` switches branches. `git checkout -- <file>` discards changes. `git switch` is a newer command specifically for switching branches.

Q86. What is operator overloading?
A) Defining multiple functions with the same name
B) Allowing operators (like +, -, *) to have different meanings for different data types (especially user-defined types)
C) Optimizing operator performance
D) Hiding operators
Answer: B
Explanation: Languages like C++ allow operators to be redefined for custom classes.

Q87. Which graph representation is typically more space-efficient for sparse graphs?
A) Adjacency Matrix
B) Adjacency List
C) Incidence Matrix
D) Edge List
Answer: B
Explanation: Adjacency lists only store existing edges (O(V+E) space), whereas matrices store entries for all possible edges (O(V^2) space).

Q88. What is the role of the 'constructor' in OOP?
A) To destroy an object
B) A special method used to initialize a newly created object
C) To perform calculations
D) To define static variables
Answer: B
Explanation: Constructors are called when an object is instantiated using `new`, setting up its initial state.

Q89. Which network protocol ensures reliable, ordered, and error-checked delivery of a stream of octets?
A) IP
B) UDP
C) TCP
D) ICMP
Answer: C
Explanation: TCP provides these reliability features over the less reliable IP layer.

Q90. What is 'normalization' in the context of databases?
A) Speeding up queries
B) The process of organizing data to minimize redundancy and improve data integrity
C) Creating backups
D) Granting user permissions
Answer: B
Explanation: Normalization involves structuring tables according to rules (normal forms) to reduce data duplication and anomalies.

Q91. Which search algorithm requires the data to be sorted?
A) Linear Search
B) Binary Search
C) Depth-First Search
D) Breadth-First Search
Answer: B
Explanation: Binary search works by repeatedly dividing the search interval in half, which requires the elements to be sorted.

Q92. What is the purpose of the `static` keyword in Java (when applied to a method)?
A) The method cannot be changed
B) The method belongs to the class itself, not to any specific object instance
C) The method can only be called by subclasses
D) The method is automatically executed
Answer: B
Explanation: Static methods are called using the class name (e.g., `Math.max()`) and do not operate on a specific object's state.

Q93. Which HTML tag defines a table cell?
A) `<table>`
B) `<tr>`
C) `<td>`
D) `<th>`
Answer: C
Explanation: `<td>` (table data) defines a standard data cell. `<th>` defines a header cell.

Q94. What is JSON?

D) A web server
Answer: B
Explanation: JavaScript Object Notation (JSON) is commonly used for transmitting data between a server and web application, as an alternative to XML.

Q95. Which type of SQL join returns only the rows where the join condition is met in both tables?
A) LEFT JOIN
B) RIGHT JOIN
C) FULL OUTER JOIN
D) INNER JOIN
Answer: D
Explanation: INNER JOIN selects records that have matching values in both tables.

Q96. What is the main characteristic of cache memory?
A) Large capacity
B) Low cost
C) High speed access
D) Non-volatile
Answer: C
Explanation: Cache memory is significantly faster than main memory (RAM), allowing the CPU to access frequently used data more quickly.

Q97. Which Linux command displays the manual page for another command?
A) `help`
B) `info`
C) `man`
D) `whatis`
Answer: C
Explanation: `man <command>` shows the manual (documentation) for the specified command.

Q98. In CSS, what is the difference between `class` and `id` selectors?
A) No difference
B) `class` can be used on multiple elements, `id` must be unique per page
C) `id` can be used on multiple elements, `class` must be unique
D) `class` is for styling, `id` is for scripting
Answer: B
Explanation: An `id` should uniquely identify one element, whereas a `class` can be applied to many elements to share styles.

Q99. Which automata is computationally the most powerful?
A) Finite Automaton (FA)
B) Pushdown Automaton (PDA)
C) Linear Bounded Automaton (LBA)
D) Turing Machine
Answer: D
Explanation: A Turing Machine is the theoretical model for general-purpose computation and can recognize the largest class of languages (recursively enumerable).

Q100. What does the `return` statement do in a function?
A) Starts the function execution
B) Ends the function execution and optionally sends a value back to the caller
C) Prints output to the console
D) Declares a variable
Answer: B
Explanation: `return` exits the current function and passes control back to where it was called from.

Q101. Which data structure would be best for checking balanced parentheses in an expression?
A) Queue
B) Stack
C) Linked List
D) Heap
Answer: B
Explanation: A stack can be used to push opening parentheses and pop them when the corresponding closing parenthesis is found.

Q102. In Java, what is garbage collection?
A) Manually freeing memory
B) The automatic process of reclaiming memory occupied by objects that are no longer referenced
C) Compiling code
D) Handling exceptions
Answer: B
Explanation: Java's garbage collector automatically manages memory deallocation.

Q103. What is the default subnet mask for a Class A IP address?
A) 255.0.0.0
B) 255.255.0.0
C) 255.255.255.0
D) 255.255.255.255
Answer: A
Explanation: Class A addresses use the first octet for the network and the remaining three for hosts by default.

Q104. Which testing is done by end-users at the developer's site?
A) Unit Testing
B) Integration Testing
C) Alpha Testing
D) Beta Testing
Answer: C
Explanation: Alpha testing is a form of internal acceptance testing performed before releasing the product to external testers (beta testing).

Q105. What does the ML term 'feature' refer to?
A) The target variable to be predicted
B) An individual measurable property or characteristic of the data being observed
C) The algorithm used for training
D) The evaluation metric
Answer: B
Explanation: Features are the input variables used by the machine learning model to make predictions.

Q106. Which logic gate is represented by the '+' symbol in Boolean algebra (usually)?
A) AND
B) OR
C) NOT
D) XOR
Answer: B
Explanation: The '+' symbol typically denotes the logical OR operation. ('.' denotes AND).

Q107. Latency in a network refers to:
A) The maximum data rate
B) The delay in data transmission from source to destination
C) The amount of data lost
D) The number of connected devices
Answer: B
Explanation: Latency is the time it takes for a data packet to travel from one point to another.

Q108. Which SQL statement is used to delete a database?
A) `DELETE DATABASE database_name;`
B) `REMOVE DATABASE database_name;`
C) `DROP DATABASE database_name;`
D) `TRUNCATE DATABASE database_name;`
Answer: C
Explanation: `DROP DATABASE` permanently removes an entire database.

Q109. Which condition must hold for deadlock? I. Mutual Exclusion II. Hold and Wait III. No Preemption IV. Circular Wait
A) I and II only
B) I, II, and III only
C) II, III, and IV only
D) All I, II, III, and IV
Answer: D
Explanation: All four Coffman conditions must hold simultaneously for a deadlock to occur.

Q110. What is the main difference between DFS and BFS?
A) DFS uses a queue, BFS uses a stack
B) BFS uses a queue, DFS uses a stack (or recursion)
C) DFS finds the shortest path, BFS does not
D) BFS is faster for all graphs
Answer: B
Explanation: BFS explores level by level using a queue, while DFS explores branch by branch using a stack (implicitly via recursion or explicitly).

Q111. Which HTML tag is used to include external JavaScript code?
A) `<javascript>`
B) `<script src="file.js">`
C) `<js>`
D) `<link type="text/javascript">`
Answer: B
Explanation: The `<script>` tag with the `src` attribute links to an external JavaScript file.

Q112. What is the role of HTTP cookies?
A) To store large files
B) To allow the server to store small pieces of information on the client's browser for session management or tracking
C) To encrypt data
D) To style web pages
Answer: B
Explanation: Cookies help maintain state over the stateless HTTP protocol.

Q113. What does 'push' mean in the context of Git?
A) To download changes from a remote repository
B) To upload local repository commits to a remote repository
C) To discard local changes
D) To create a new branch
Answer: B
Explanation: `git push` sends your committed changes to a remote server (like GitHub).

Q114. Which algorithm is used for linear regression?
A) K-Means
B) Gradient Descent (to find coefficients)
C) Apriori
D) Decision Tree
Answer: B
Explanation: Gradient descent is commonly used to iteratively adjust the model parameters (coefficients) to minimize the error (e.g., Mean Squared Error) in linear regression.

Q115. Which protocol provides secure communication over the internet, forming the basis of HTTPS?
A) HTTP
B) FTP
C) SMTP
D) TLS/SSL
Answer: D
Explanation: Transport Layer Security (TLS) and its predecessor Secure Sockets Layer (SSL) encrypt HTTP communication.

Q116. What is the function of the operating system's 'shell'?
A) Manages memory allocation
B) Provides a command-line interface (CLI) or graphical user interface (GUI) for users to interact with the OS
C) Performs CPU scheduling
D) Handles device drivers
Answer: B
Explanation: The shell acts as an interpreter between the user and the kernel.

Q117. What is the octal equivalent of the binary number 110101?
A) 55
B) 65
C) 75
D) 53
Answer: B
Explanation: Group binary digits in threes from the right: (110)(101). Convert each group: 110 = 6, 101 = 5. So, 65 in octal.

Q118. Which CSS property is used to make text bold?
A) `font-style`
B) `text-decoration`
C) `font-weight`
D) `text-transform`
Answer: C
Explanation: `font-weight: bold;` or `font-weight: 700;` makes text bold.

Q119. What is an 'abstract method' in OOP?
A) A method with a default implementation
B) A method declared without an implementation (body), which must be implemented by subclasses
C) A static method
D) A private method
Answer: B
Explanation: Abstract methods define a method signature but leave the implementation details to concrete subclasses.

Q120. Which type of database join is typically the most expensive in terms of computation?
A) INNER JOIN
B) LEFT JOIN
C) CROSS JOIN (Cartesian Product)
D) Self Join
Answer: C
Explanation: A CROSS JOIN generates all possible combinations of rows from the joined tables, which can be very large and resource-intensive if the tables are not small.

Q121. What does the `traceroute` (or `tracert`) command do?
A) Measures bandwidth
B) Pings a host continuously
C) Shows the network path (hops) taken by packets to reach a destination host
D) Displays the ARP table
Answer: C
Explanation: `traceroute` helps diagnose network connectivity issues by identifying the routers along the path.

Q122. Which algorithm technique is used in the Floyd-Warshall algorithm?
A) Greedy
B) Divide and Conquer
C) Dynamic Programming
D) Backtracking
Answer: C
Explanation: Floyd-Warshall uses dynamic programming to iteratively find the shortest paths between all pairs of vertices.

Q123. In Python, what does `str(123)` do?
A) Causes an error
B) Converts the integer 123 to the string "123"
C) Calculates the length of 123
D) Converts "123" to an integer
Answer: B
Explanation: The `str()` function converts various data types into their string representation.

Q124. What is Cross-Site Request Forgery (CSRF)?
A) Injecting scripts into a website
B) Overwhelming a server with requests
C) Tricking a user's browser into making an unintended, malicious request to a web application they are authenticated with
D) Intercepting network traffic
Answer: C
Explanation: CSRF exploits the trust a web application has in an authenticated user's browser.

Q125. What is the purpose of RAID (Redundant Array of Independent Disks)?
A) To increase CPU speed
B) To provide data redundancy, improve performance, or both by combining multiple disk drives
C) To manage virtual memory
D) To encrypt data
Answer: B
Explanation: Different RAID levels offer trade-offs between fault tolerance (redundancy) and speed (performance).

Q126. Which data structure is used to manage function calls and local variables during program execution?
A) Heap
B) Queue
C) Call Stack
D) Hash Table
Answer: C
Explanation: The call stack keeps track of active function calls, their parameters, and local variables.

Q127. In object-oriented design, what is composition?
A) An "is-a" relationship (inheritance)
B) A "has-a" relationship, where an object contains instances of other objects
C) Making methods abstract
D) Overloading operators
Answer: B
Explanation: Composition allows building complex objects by combining simpler ones, favoring flexibility over rigid inheritance hierarchies.

Q128. What is the maximum number of hosts available on a network with subnet mask 255.255.255.0?
A) 256
B) 255
C) 254
D) 128
Answer: C
Explanation: 255.255.255.0 leaves 8 bits for the host portion (2^8 = 256 addresses). Subtracting the network address and the broadcast address leaves 254 usable host addresses.

Q129. What is 'refactoring' in software development?
A) Adding new features
B) Fixing bugs
C) Restructuring existing computer code without changing its external behavior, to improve nonfunctional attributes
D) Writing documentation
Answer: C
Explanation: Refactoring aims to improve code readability, maintainability, and design quality.

Q130. Which machine learning task involves predicting a continuous value?
A) Classification
B) Regression
C) Clustering
D) Dimensionality Reduction
Answer: B
Explanation: Regression models predict numerical outcomes (e.g., house price, temperature). Classification predicts categories.

Q131. Which Boolean operation corresponds to the intersection of sets?
A) OR
B) AND
C) NOT
D) XOR
Answer: B
Explanation: Logical AND corresponds to set intersection (elements present in both sets). OR corresponds to union.

Q132. Which network command on Windows displays the IP configuration?
A) `ifconfig`
B) `ipconfig`
C) `netstat`
D) `ping`
Answer: B
Explanation: `ipconfig` shows details like IP address, subnet mask, and default gateway. (`ifconfig` is common on Linux/Unix).

Q133. What is the goal of the Third Normal Form (3NF) in database normalization?
A) Eliminate repeating groups
B) Eliminate partial dependencies
C) Eliminate transitive dependencies
D) Eliminate all redundancy
Answer: C
Explanation: 3NF requires a table to be in 2NF and ensures that non-prime attributes are directly dependent only on the primary key, not on other non-prime attributes.

Q134. What is Belady's Anomaly?
A) A situation in CPU scheduling where adding more CPUs slows down execution
B) A situation in page replacement algorithms where increasing the number of page frames results in an increase in the number of page faults
C) A type of network congestion
D) A file system error
Answer: B
Explanation: This counter-intuitive behavior can occur with algorithms like FIFO.

Q135. What algorithm might be used to find the shortest path in a maze?
A) Quick Sort
B) Prim's Algorithm
C) Breadth-First Search (BFS)
D) Heapify
Answer: C
Explanation: BFS can be adapted to find the shortest path in terms of steps in an unweighted grid or graph like a maze.

Q136. Which HTML tag defines metadata about the HTML document (e.g., character set, viewport)?

B) `<meta>`
C) `<title>`
D) `<header>`
Answer: B
Explanation: `<meta>` tags are placed within the `<head>` section and provide information not directly displayed on the page.

Q137. What is 'event delegation' in JavaScript?
A) Assigning events directly to child elements
B) Using a single event listener on a parent element to manage events for multiple child elements
C) Preventing events from happening
D) Creating custom events
Answer: B
Explanation: Event delegation leverages event bubbling and improves performance by reducing the number of listeners.

Q138. Which Git command is used to merge changes from another branch into the current branch?

Explanation: `git merge <branch_name>` integrates changes from the specified branch into the currently checked-out branch.

Q139. What is 'gradient descent' in machine learning?

B) An optimization algorithm used to minimize a function (like a loss function) by iteratively moving in the direction of steepest descent
C) A data visualization technique
D) A feature scaling method
Answer: B
Explanation: It's a fundamental algorithm for training many machine learning models, especially neural networks.

Q140. Which security principle involves validating user inputs to prevent attacks like SQL injection or XSS?
A) Least Privilege
B) Defense in Depth
C) Input Validation/Sanitization
D) Fail-Safe Defaults
Answer: C
Explanation: Properly validating and sanitizing all external inputs is crucial for preventing injection attacks.

Q141. What is the output of `(void*)0 == NULL` in C?
A) 0 (false)
B) 1 (true)
C) Compiler dependent
D) Compiler error
Answer: B
Explanation: NULL is typically defined as `(void*)0`, so the comparison evaluates to true (1).

Q142. Which data structure stores elements in sorted order and provides O(log n) search, insert, and delete?
A) Hash Table
B) Linked List
C) Balanced Binary Search Tree (AVL, Red-Black)
D) Queue
Answer: C
Explanation: Balanced BSTs maintain sorted order while ensuring logarithmic time complexity for core operations.

Q143. In process management, what is a 'thread'?

C) A system call
D) A memory segment
Answer: B
Explanation: Threads allow for concurrent execution paths within a single process, sharing memory space.

Q144. What does the HTTP status code 301 indicate?

Q145. Which SQL function returns the current date and time?

Answer: C
Explanation: The exact function name varies (e.g., `NOW()` in MySQL/PostgreSQL, `GETDATE()` in SQL Server), but databases provide functions for the current timestamp.

Q146. What does 'endianness' refer to?
A) CPU clock speed
B) The order in which bytes are arranged in computer memory for multi-byte data types
C) Network transmission speed
D) File system block size
Answer: B
Explanation: It determines whether the most significant byte (Big Endian) or least significant byte (Little Endian) is stored at the lowest memory address.

Q147. Which phase of compilation translates intermediate code into target machine code?

Q149. What is 'regression' in machine learning?

B) Predicting a continuous numerical value

Answer: B
Explanation: Regression models aim to predict quantities like price, temperature, or count.

Q150. Which layer of the OSI model provides the interface for applications to access network services?
A) Application Layer
B) Presentation Layer
C) Session Layer
D) Transport Layer
Answer: A
Explanation: The Application Layer contains protocols that applications use directly (e.g., HTTP, SMTP, FTP).

Q151. What is the value of the hexadecimal number FF in decimal?
A) 15
B) 16
C) 255
D) 256
Answer: C
Explanation: FF (hex) = (15 * 16^1) + (15 * 16^0) = 240 + 15 = 255.

Q152. Which CSS selector targets all `<p>` elements?
A) `#p`
B) `.p`
C) `p`
D) `*p`
Answer: C
Explanation: Using the tag name directly selects all elements of that type.

Q153. What is the primary key constraint used for?
A) To enforce uniqueness and provide an identifier for rows in a table
B) To link tables together
C) To allow NULL values
D) To sort data
Answer: A
Explanation: It ensures each row can be uniquely identified and prevents NULLs.

Q154. Which type of scheduling involves the OS forcibly taking the CPU away from a process?
A) Non-preemptive scheduling
B) Preemptive scheduling
C) FCFS scheduling
D) Batch scheduling
Answer: B
Explanation: Preemptive schedulers can interrupt a running process to allocate the CPU to another, often higher-priority, process.

Q155. What data structure does Dijkstra's algorithm often use to efficiently select the next node to visit?
A) Stack
B) Queue
C) Priority Queue (Min-Heap)
D) Hash Table
Answer: C
Explanation: A priority queue allows efficient retrieval of the unvisited node with the smallest known distance.

Q156. In Python, which collection type stores unordered items and does not allow duplicates?
A) List
B) Tuple
C) Dictionary
D) Set
Answer: D
Explanation: Sets store unique elements in an unordered fashion.

Q157. Which security attack floods a network with ICMP echo requests?
A) SYN Flood
B) Smurf Attack
C) Teardrop Attack
D) SQL Injection
Answer: B
Explanation: A Smurf attack involves sending ICMP echo requests to a broadcast address with the victim's spoofed IP, causing many hosts to reply to the victim.

Q158. What is the 'this' pointer in C++?
A) A pointer to the superclass
B) A pointer available within non-static member functions that points to the object itself
C) A pointer to global variables
D) A null pointer
Answer: B
Explanation: `this` provides access to the current object's members within its methods.

Q159. Which type of file access allows reading or writing data anywhere in the file?
A) Sequential Access
B) Random Access (Direct Access)
C) Indexed Access
D) Buffered Access
Answer: B
Explanation: Random access allows accessing any part of the file directly without reading through preceding data.

Q160. What does MVC stand for in software architecture?
A) Model-View-Controller
B) Method-Variable-Class
C) Main-View-Component
D) Model-Verify-Compile
Answer: A
Explanation: MVC is a common architectural pattern separating application logic (Model), user interface (View), and input handling (Controller).

Q161. Which machine learning concept deals with a model's ability to perform well on unseen data?
A) Training Error
B) Bias
C) Variance
D) Generalization
Answer: D
Explanation: Generalization refers to how well a model trained on a specific dataset performs on new, previously unseen data from the same distribution.

Q162. A flip-flop is an example of which type of digital circuit?
A) Combinational Logic
B) Sequential Logic
C) Arithmetic Logic
D) Analog Circuit
Answer: B
Explanation: Sequential circuits have memory elements (like flip-flops) and their output depends on current inputs and past states. Combinational outputs depend only on current inputs.

Q13. What is the difference between latency and throughput?
A) No difference
B) Latency is delay, Throughput is data rate
C) Latency is data rate, Throughput is delay
D) Latency is error rate, Throughput is delay
Answer: B
Explanation: Latency measures the time delay for data transfer, while throughput measures the amount of data transferred per unit time.

Q164. What is the purpose of the `GROUP BY` clause in SQL?
A) To sort the result set
B) To filter rows
C) To group rows that have the same values in specified columns into summary rows, often for aggregate functions
D) To join tables
Answer: C
Explanation: `GROUP BY` collapses multiple rows with common values into a single summary row.

Q165. What is 'swapping' in operating systems?
A) Moving processes between main memory and secondary storage (disk)
B) Exchanging data between registers
C) Replacing pages in memory
D) Scheduling processes
Answer: A
Explanation: Swapping allows the OS to run more processes than can fit in physical RAM simultaneously by temporarily moving inactive processes to disk.

Q166. Which data structure is best for finding the median in a stream of numbers efficiently?
A) Single Sorted Array
B) Two Heaps (Min-Heap and Max-Heap)
C) Hash Table
D) Stack
Answer: B
Explanation: Maintaining a max-heap for the lower half and a min-heap for the upper half allows finding the median in O(log n) insertion time and O(1) query time.

Q167. How do you declare an integer variable 'age' in Java?

Answer: B
Explanation: Java uses the syntax `DataType variableName;`.

Q168. Which HTTP header is used by the client to specify the desired media types for the response?

Q170. Which ML evaluation metric is calculated as TP / (TP + FP)?

Q174. In C++, what is a 'reference' (&)?

Q175. Which network topology involves connecting computers along a single cable?

Q176. Which sorting algorithm has a time complexity of O(n^2) in all cases (worst, average, best)?

B) Insertion Sort
C) Selection Sort
D) Quick Sort
Answer: C
Explanation: Selection sort always scans the unsorted portion to find the minimum/maximum, resulting in O(n^2) comparisons regardless of input order.

Q177. What is 'dead code' in programming?

B) Code that is executed but has no effect on the program's output or state
C) Code that is never executed (unreachable code)
D) Commented-out code
Answer: C
Explanation: Dead code (unreachable code) can often be removed by optimizers. (Sometimes B is also considered dead code).

Q178. Which SQL keyword specifies the table(s) to retrieve data from?

Q179. What is context switching in operating systems?

C) Translating virtual addresses
D) Handling interrupts
Answer: B
Explanation: Context switching is essential for multitasking, allowing the CPU to switch between different tasks.

Q180. Which data structure is well-suited for implementing Breadth-First Search (BFS)?

Q184. In machine learning, what does 'k' represent in k-Nearest Neighbors (k-NN)?

Q185. What is the main principle behind asymmetric (public-key) cryptography?

Q190. What is 'inheritance' in database modeling (though not directly supported in standard SQL)?

Q191. Which condition causes a 'segmentation fault'?

Q192. Which graph algorithm finds the shortest paths from a single source vertex to all other vertices in a weighted graph?

Explanation: Dijkstra's algorithm is designed for the single-source shortest path problem on graphs with non-negative edge weights.

Q193. What is the difference between `List` and `Tuple` in Python?

Q195. What is 'responsive web design'?

Q196. Which SQL statement modifies the structure of an existing table?
