B) `UPDATE TABLE`
C) `ALTER TABLE`
D) `MODIFY TABLE`
Answer: C
Explanation: `ALTER TABLE` is used to add, delete, or modify columns, or change constraints.

Q197. Which type of attack aims to make a machine or network resource unavailable to its intended users?
A) Phishing
B) Man-in-the-Middle
C) Denial-of-Service (DoS)
D) Malware infection
Answer: C
Explanation: DoS attacks typically flood the target with traffic or requests to overwhelm it.

Q198. What is the function of the BIOS/UEFI?
A) To run application software
B) To manage files on the hard drive
C) To initialize hardware during the boot process and load the operating system
D) To provide network connectivity
Answer: C
Explanation: Basic Input/Output System (BIOS) or Unified Extensible Firmware Interface (UEFI) is the firmware that starts the computer.

Q199. What does 'Big O' notation describe?
A) The exact running time of an algorithm
B) The best-case performance of an algorithm
C) The upper bound of the growth rate of an algorithm's resource usage (time or space) as input size increases
D) The average memory usage
Answer: C
Explanation: Big O provides an asymptotic upper bound on complexity.

Q200. Which language is commonly used for defining the structure and content of web pages?
A) CSS
B) JavaScript
C) HTML
D) Python
Answer: C
Explanation: HyperText Markup Language (HTML) is the standard markup language for creating web page structure.


SET 11 (BEL)

Q1. A train running at the speed of 60 km/hr crosses a pole in 9 seconds. What is the length of the train?
A) 120 metres
B) 180 metres
C) 324 metres
D) 150 metres
Answer: D
Explanation: Speed = 60 km/hr = 60 * (5/18) m/s = 50/3 m/s. Length = Speed * Time = (50/3) * 9 = 150 metres.

Q2. Find the greatest number that will divide 43, 91 and 183 so as to leave the same remainder in each case.
A) 4
B) 7
C) 9
D) 13
Answer: A
Explanation: Required number = HCF of (91-43), (183-91), (183-43) = HCF of 48, 92, 140. HCF(48, 92, 140) = 4.

Q3. The ratio of two numbers is 3:4 and their LCM is 120. The sum of the numbers is:
A) 70
B) 140
C) 35
D) 105
Answer: A
Explanation: Let numbers be 3x and 4x. LCM = 12x. 12x = 120 => x = 10. Numbers are 30 and 40. Sum = 30 + 40 = 70.

Q4. If log 2 = 0.30103, the number of digits in 2^64 is:
A) 19
B) 20
C) 21
D) 22
Answer: B
Explanation: log(2^64) = 64 * log 2 = 64 * 0.30103 = 19.26592. The number of digits is the characteristic (integer part) + 1 = 19 + 1 = 20.

Q5. A vendor bought toffees at 6 for a rupee. How many for a rupee must he sell to gain 20%?
A) 3
B) 4
C) 5
D) None of these
Answer: C
Explanation: Cost Price (CP) of 6 toffees = Re 1. CP of 1 toffee = Re 1/6. Selling Price (SP) for 20% gain = CP * (1 + Gain%) = (1/6) * (1 + 0.20) = (1/6) * 1.2 = (1/6) * (6/5) = Re 1/5. So, he must sell 5 toffees for Re 1.

Q6. What was the day of the week on 15th August 1947?
A) Thursday
B) Friday
C) Saturday
D) Sunday
Answer: B
Explanation: Calculate odd days: 1900 years -> 1 odd day. 46 years (1901-1946) -> 11 leap years, 35 ordinary years -> (11*2 + 35*1) = 22 + 35 = 57 days = 1 odd day. Days in 1947 till Aug 15: Jan(3)+Feb(0)+Mar(3)+Apr(2)+May(3)+Jun(2)+Jul(3)+Aug(15) = 31 days = 3 odd days. Total odd days = 1 + 1 + 3 = 5. Day 5 is Friday.

Q7. Find the average of first 40 natural numbers.
A) 18.5
B) 19.5
C) 20.5
D) 21.5
Answer: C
Explanation: Sum of first n natural numbers = n(n+1)/2. Sum = 40(41)/2 = 820. Average = Sum / n = 820 / 40 = 20.5.

Q8. Simple interest on a certain sum of money for 3 years at 8% per annum is half the compound interest on Rs. 4000 for 2 years at 10% per annum. The sum placed on simple interest is:
A) Rs. 1550
B) Rs. 1650
C) Rs. 1750
D) Rs. 2000
Answer: C
Explanation: CI on Rs 4000 = 4000 * (1 + 10/100)^2 - 4000 = 4000 * (1.1)^2 - 4000 = 4840 - 4000 = Rs 840. SI = Half of CI = 840 / 2 = Rs 420. Sum (P) = (SI * 100) / (R * T) = (420 * 100) / (8 * 3) = 42000 / 24 = Rs 1750.

Q9. Look at this series: 36, 34, 30, 28, 24, ... What number should come next?
A) 20
B) 22
C) 23
D) 26
Answer: B
Explanation: The pattern is -2, -4, -2, -4, ... The next step is -2. So, 24 - 2 = 22.

Q10. How many times are the hands of a clock at right angles in a day?
A) 22
B) 24
C) 44
D) 48
Answer: C
Explanation: In 12 hours, the hands are at right angles 22 times. In 24 hours, they are at right angles 44 times.

Q11. Find the next term: 1, 1, 2, 3, 5, 8, ?
A) 11
B) 13
C) 15
D) 17
Answer: B
Explanation: This is the Fibonacci sequence, where each term is the sum of the two preceding ones. 5 + 8 = 13.

Q12. If South-East becomes North, North-East becomes West and so on. What will West become?
A) North-East
B) North-West
C) South-East
D) South-West
Answer: C
Explanation: The directions are rotated 135 degrees counter-clockwise. West rotated 135 degrees counter-clockwise becomes South-East.

Q13. Choose the alternative which is closely resembles the mirror image of the given combination: QUALITY
A) YTILAИỌ
B) YTILAՍỌ
C) YTILAUQ
D) YTİLAUQ
Answer: C
Explanation: The mirror image reverses the letters: Y T I L A U Q. Horizontal flipping of individual letters is usually ignored in simple text representation.

Q14. If A+B means A is the brother of B; A-B means A is the sister of B and A*B means A is the father of B. Which of the following means that C is the son of M?
A) M - N * C + F
B) F - C + N * M
C) N + M - F * C
D) M * N - C + F
Answer: D
Explanation: M * N -> M is father of N. N - C -> N is sister of C. C + F -> C is brother of F. From M*N and N-C, M is father to siblings N and C. Since C is a brother (C+F), C is the son of M.

Q15. Find the odd word: Monitor, Keyboard, Mouse, Webcam
A) Monitor
B) Keyboard
C) Mouse
D) Webcam
Answer: A
Explanation: Keyboard, Mouse, and Webcam are input devices. Monitor is an output device.

Q16. Arrange the words: 1. Nation, 2. Village, 3. City, 4. District, 5. State
A) 2, 3, 4, 5, 1
B) 2, 4, 5, 3, 1
C) 1, 3, 5, 4, 2
D) 2, 4, 3, 5, 1
Answer: A
Explanation: The logical order from smallest to largest administrative/geographical unit is: Village -> City -> District -> State -> Nation. So, 2, 3, 4, 5, 1. (Assuming city generally larger than village, district larger than city).

Q17. Choose the pair that has a similar relationship to Doctor : Diagnosis.
A) Teacher : School
B) Judge : Judgement
C) Thief : Prison
D) Politician : Votes
Answer: B
Explanation: A Doctor performs a Diagnosis. A Judge delivers a Judgement.

Q18. Choose the missing number: 8, 27, 64, ?, 216
A) 100
B) 125
C) 150
D) 196
Answer: B
Explanation: The series consists of cubes of consecutive integers: 2^3, 3^3, 4^3, 5^3, 6^3. The missing term is 5^3 = 125.

Q19. Introducing a boy, a girl said, "He is the son of the daughter of the father of my uncle." How is the boy related to the girl?
A) Brother
B) Nephew
C) Uncle
D) Son-in-law
Answer: A
Explanation: "Father of my uncle" = grandfather. "Daughter of grandfather" = mother or aunt. "Son of mother/aunt" = brother or cousin. 'Brother' is the most plausible direct relationship given the options.

Q20. What number should come next? 7, 10, 8, 11, 9, 12, ?
A) 7
B) 10
C) 12
D) 13
Answer: B
Explanation: This is an alternating series. One series starts at 7 and increases by 1: 7, 8, 9, 10. The other starts at 10 and increases by 1: 10, 11, 12. The next term is from the first series.

Q21. Statement: Should income tax be abolished in India? Arguments: I. Yes. It is an unnecessary burden on the wage earners. II. No. It is a good source of revenue for the government.
A) Only argument I is strong
B) Only argument II is strong
C) Either I or II is strong
D) Both I and II are strong
Answer: B
Explanation: Argument I is weak as taxation is necessary. Argument II provides a strong reason (revenue source) against abolishing income tax.

Q22. Select the pair which is different: (Painter : Brush), (Carpenter : Saw), (Doctor : Stethoscope), (Mason : Wall)
A) Painter : Brush
B) Carpenter : Saw
C) Doctor : Stethoscope
D) Mason : Wall
Answer: D
Explanation: Brush, Saw, and Stethoscope are tools. Wall is the product made by the Mason.

Q23. If CAR is 22, BUS is 43, what is TRUCK? (Using A=1...Z=26)
A) 65
B) 73
C) 85
D) 95
Answer: B
Explanation: Sum of letter positions: C(3)+A(1)+R(18)=22. B(2)+U(21)+S(19)=42. (The question likely has a typo for BUS, it should be 42 or the coding is different). Assuming standard sum: TRUCK = T(20)+R(18)+U(21)+C(3)+K(11) = 73.

Q24. Choose the figure which is different from the rest. (Assume shapes: Square, Circle, Triangle, Pentagon)
A) Square
B) Circle
C) Triangle
D) Pentagon
Answer: B
Explanation: Square, Triangle, Pentagon are polygons (made of straight lines). Circle is a curve.

Q25. A watch reads 4:30. If the minute hand points East, in what direction will the hour hand point?
A) North
B) North-West
C) South-East
D) North-East
Answer: D
Explanation: At 4:30, minute hand is at 6 (East). Hour hand is halfway between 4 and 5. If 6 is East, 3 is North, 12 is West. The position between 4 and 5 is North-East.

Q26. Which operator in C is used to access the value stored at an address pointed to by a pointer?
A) & (Address-of)
B) * (Dereference/Indirection)
C) -> (Arrow)
D) . (Dot)
Answer: B
Explanation: The dereference operator `*` retrieves the value located at the memory address stored in the pointer variable.

Q27. What is the difference between `malloc()` and `calloc()` in C?
A) `malloc()` allocates multiple blocks, `calloc()` allocates a single block
B) `malloc()` initializes memory to zero, `calloc()` does not
C) `calloc()` allocates memory and initializes it to zero, `malloc()` allocates memory but does not initialize it
D) No difference, they are synonyms
Answer: C
Explanation: `calloc` takes number of elements and size, initializes to zero. `malloc` takes total bytes, content is uninitialized.

Q28. What is the output of the following C code?
#include <stdio.h>
int main() { int a=5, b=7; printf("%d", a+++b); return 0; }
A) 12
B) 13
C) 11
D) Compiler Error/Undefined
Answer: A
Explanation: `a++ + b` uses the original value of `a` (5) for the addition, then increments `a`. So, 5 + 7 = 12 is printed. `a` becomes 6 afterwards.

Q29. Which C standard library header file is needed for string manipulation functions like `strcpy`, `strlen`?
A) `<stdio.h>`
B) `<stdlib.h>`
C) `<string.h>`
D) `<math.h>`
Answer: C
Explanation: `<string.h>` contains declarations for functions operating on null-terminated character arrays (strings).

Q30. Which data structure is suitable for representing a hierarchical structure, like a file system?
A) Queue
B) Stack
C) Tree
D) Hash Table
Answer: C
Explanation: Trees naturally model hierarchical parent-child relationships found in file systems or organization charts.

Q31. Which algorithm finds the shortest path between all pairs of vertices in a weighted graph?
A) Dijkstra's Algorithm
B) Prim's Algorithm
C) Floyd-Warshall Algorithm
D) Breadth-First Search
Answer: C
Explanation: Floyd-Warshall is a dynamic programming algorithm designed for the all-pairs shortest path problem, handling negative edges (but not negative cycles).

Q32. What is the time complexity of the bubble sort algorithm in the worst case?
A) O(n)
B) O(log n)
C) O(n log n)
D) O(n^2)
Answer: D
Explanation: In the worst case (e.g., reverse sorted array), bubble sort requires comparing and potentially swapping adjacent elements across multiple passes, leading to O(n^2) complexity.

Q33. Which data structure stores elements based on key-value pairs?
A) Stack
B) Queue
C) Hash Map (or Dictionary)
D) Linked List
Answer: C
Explanation: Hash maps, dictionaries, or associative arrays are designed to store and retrieve values associated with unique keys.

Q34. Which algorithm paradigm does Prim's algorithm for finding MST belong to?
A) Divide and Conquer
B) Dynamic Programming
C) Greedy Algorithm
D) Backtracking
Answer: C
Explanation: Prim's algorithm greedily adds the minimum-weight edge connecting a vertex in the growing MST to a vertex outside it.

Q35. What defines a "complete" binary tree?
A) Every node has exactly two children
B) All levels are completely filled except possibly the last level, which is filled from left to right
C) The tree is perfectly balanced
D) All leaf nodes are at the same depth
Answer: B
Explanation: This specific definition distinguishes a complete binary tree, important for heap implementations.

Q36. What is the purpose of memoization in dynamic programming?
A) To sort the data
B) To store the results of expensive function calls (subproblems) and return the cached result when the same inputs occur again
C) To choose the best option locally
D) To traverse a graph
Answer: B
Explanation: Memoization (top-down DP) avoids redundant computations by caching subproblem results.

Q37. Which process state indicates the process has finished execution?
A) New
B) Ready
C) Running
D) Terminated
Answer: D
Explanation: The Terminated state signifies that the process has completed its task.

Q38. What is the role of the `exec()` family of system calls in Unix/Linux?
A) To create a new process
B) To replace the current process image with a new program
C) To wait for a child process to terminate
D) To send a signal to a process
Answer: B
Explanation: `exec()` loads and runs a new program within the context of the existing process.

Q39. What does a page table typically store?
A) Process control blocks
B) Mappings between virtual page numbers and physical frame numbers
C) File system metadata
D) CPU register values
Answer: B
Explanation: The page table is the data structure used by the MMU to translate virtual addresses generated by a process into physical addresses in RAM.

Q40. Which scheduling algorithm is designed for real-time systems to meet deadlines?
A) FCFS
B) SJF
C) Round Robin
D) Earliest Deadline First (EDF) or Rate Monotonic (RM)
Answer: D
Explanation: Real-time scheduling algorithms like EDF and RM prioritize tasks based on their deadlines or periods to ensure timely execution.

Q41. What is the primary cause of external fragmentation?
A) Fixed-size memory blocks (paging)
B) Variable-size memory blocks being allocated and freed over time, leaving small, unusable gaps between allocated blocks
C) Processes using less memory than allocated within a block
D) Excessive page swapping
Answer: B
Explanation: External fragmentation occurs with dynamic or segmented memory allocation schemes.

Q42. Which layer of the TCP/IP model handles physical addressing (MAC addresses)?
A) Application Layer
B) Transport Layer
C) Internet Layer
D) Network Access Layer (Link Layer)
Answer: D
Explanation: The Link Layer deals with communication on the local physical network, including MAC addressing and framing.

Q43. Which command-line utility is used to query DNS servers?
A) `ping`
B) `traceroute`
C) `ipconfig` / `ifconfig`
D) `nslookup` or `dig`
Answer: D
Explanation: `nslookup` and `dig` are used to find DNS records associated with domain names.

Q44. What is the three-way handshake used for in TCP?
A) To terminate a connection
B) To establish a reliable connection between client and server
C) To handle congestion control
D) To resolve IP addresses
Answer: B
Explanation: The SYN, SYN-ACK, ACK sequence ensures both client and server are ready to communicate reliably.

Q45. What is the loopback IP address?
A) 0.0.0.0
B) 255.255.255.255
C) 192.168.1.1
D) 127.0.0.1
Answer: D
Explanation: 127.0.0.1 (usually mapped to `localhost`) refers to the current machine, used for network testing and local services.

Q46. Which network device forwards data packets between computer networks?
A) Hub
B) Switch
C) Router
D) Modem
Answer: C
Explanation: Routers operate at the Network Layer (Layer 3) and use IP addresses to direct traffic between different networks.

Q47. Which SQL keyword is used to sort the result set of a query?
A) SORT BY
B) ORDER BY
C) GROUP BY
D) ARRANGE BY
Answer: B
Explanation: `ORDER BY column_name [ASC|DESC]` sorts the output rows.

Q48. What is a 'tuple' in the context of a relational database?
A) A column in a table
B) A row in a table (a single record)
C) The entire table
D) A database constraint
Answer: B
Explanation: Tuple is the formal term for a row or record in a relation (table).

Q49. Which ACID property ensures that the effects of a committed transaction persist even if the system crashes?
A) Atomicity
B) Consistency
C) Isolation
D) Durability
Answer: D
Explanation: Durability guarantees that once a transaction is committed, its changes are permanently stored and survive subsequent failures.

Q50. Which normal form requires that all non-prime attributes are fully functionally dependent on the primary key?
A) 1NF
B) 2NF
C) 3NF
D) BCNF
Answer: B
Explanation: 2NF builds on 1NF by removing partial dependencies, where a non-prime attribute depends on only part of a composite primary key.

Q51. What is the purpose of the SQL `HAVING` clause?
A) To filter individual rows before grouping
B) To sort the final result set
C) To filter groups based on a specified condition after aggregation
D) To specify the tables to query from
Answer: C
Explanation: `HAVING` works like `WHERE`, but it operates on the results of aggregate functions applied to groups created by `GROUP BY`.

Q52. Which type of processor architecture uses a large set of complex instructions?
A) RISC (Reduced Instruction Set Computer)
B) CISC (Complex Instruction Set Computer)
C) ARM
D) MIPS
Answer: B
Explanation: CISC architectures (like traditional x86) have instructions that can perform complex, multi-step operations.

Q53. What is 'locality of reference'?
A) The physical location of memory chips
B) The tendency of processors to access the same set of memory locations repetitively over a short period (temporal locality) or access locations near recently accessed ones (spatial locality)
C) A method for routing network packets
D) A database indexing technique
Answer: B
Explanation: Locality of reference is the principle that makes caching effective.

Q54. What is the function of a bus in computer architecture?
A) Performs calculations
B) Stores data permanently
C) A communication pathway used to transfer data between different components (CPU, memory, I/O devices)
D) Executes instructions
Answer: C
Explanation: Buses are collections of wires that transmit data, addresses, and control signals.

Q55. What does 'SIMD' stand for in parallel processing?
A) Single Instruction, Multiple Data
B) Single Instruction, Multiple Devices
C) Simple Instruction, Many Devices
D) Synchronous Instruction, Master Data
Answer: A
Explanation: SIMD allows a single instruction to operate on multiple data elements simultaneously, common in multimedia and scientific computing.

Q56. Which logic gate produces an output that is the inverse of its input?
A) AND
B) OR
C) NOT
D) XOR
Answer: C
Explanation: The NOT gate is an inverter.

Q57. Represent the decimal number 13 in binary.
A) 1011
B) 1110
C) 1101
D) 1001
Answer: C
Explanation: 13 = 8 + 4 + 1 = (1 * 2^3) + (1 * 2^2) + (0 * 2^1) + (1 * 2^0), which is 1101.

Q58. Which compiler phase involves checking type compatibility and variable declarations?
A) Lexical Analysis
B) Syntax Analysis
C) Semantic Analysis
D) Code Generation
Answer: C
Explanation: Semantic Analysis verifies the meaning and consistency of the code beyond just its grammatical structure, including type checking.

Q59. What is 'assembly language'?
A) Machine language
B) A high-level language like Python
C) A low-level symbolic language that corresponds closely to machine language instructions
D) A scripting language
Answer: C
Explanation: Assembly language uses mnemonics for machine instructions, making it slightly more human-readable than raw binary code.

Q60. Which part of the compiler manages information about identifiers like their type and scope?
A) Parser
B) Lexer
C) Code Generator
D) Symbol Table Manager
Answer: D
Explanation: The symbol table is a crucial data structure used throughout compilation to store metadata about identifiers.

Q61. What type of language can be recognized by a Pushdown Automaton (PDA)?
A) Regular Languages
B) Context-Free Languages (CFLs)
C) Context-Sensitive Languages
D) Recursively Enumerable Languages
Answer: B
Explanation: PDAs have a stack in addition to finite control, giving them the power to recognize CFLs (like {a^n b^n}).

Q62. What is a key characteristic of the Agile software development methodology?
A) Strict adherence to an upfront plan
B) Minimal customer involvement
C) Iterative development and responsiveness to change
D) Heavy documentation emphasis
Answer: C
Explanation: Agile methods prioritize flexibility, collaboration, and delivering working software in short cycles.

Q63. Which testing level verifies that the complete, integrated system meets specified requirements?
A) Unit Testing
B) Integration Testing
C) System Testing
D) Acceptance Testing
Answer: C
Explanation: System testing evaluates the entire system against the functional and non-functional requirements.

Q64. What does 'cohesion' refer to in software design?
A) The degree of interdependence between modules
B) The degree to which elements inside a single module belong together (functional relatedness)
C) The number of bugs in a module
D) The speed of execution
Answer: B
Explanation: High cohesion means the elements within a module have a strong, focused purpose. Low cohesion means a module does many unrelated things.

Q65. What is the purpose of software maintenance?
A) Only fixing bugs discovered after release
B) Modifying software after delivery to correct faults, improve performance, or adapt to a changed environment
C) Initial development only
D) Writing user manuals
Answer: B
Explanation: Maintenance includes corrective, adaptive, perfective, and preventive activities.

Q66. What is the time complexity of searching for an element in a balanced Binary Search Tree?
A) O(1)
B) O(log n)
C) O(n)
D) O(n log n)
Answer: B
Explanation: The height of a balanced BST is logarithmic, leading to O(log n) search time.

Q67. Which data structure typically uses pointers to connect nodes in a sequence?
A) Array
B) Linked List
C) Stack (using array)
D) Hash Table (using array)
Answer: B
Explanation: Linked lists consist of nodes containing data and pointers (references) to the next node.

Q68. What is the main difference between Kruskal's and Prim's MST algorithms?
A) Kruskal's builds the MST by adding edges; Prim's builds it by adding vertices
B) Prim's uses a greedy approach; Kruskal's does not
C) Kruskal's works on directed graphs; Prim's on undirected
D) Prim's is always faster
Answer: A
Explanation: Kruskal's sorts all edges and adds the smallest that doesn't form a cycle. Prim's grows the tree one vertex at a time from an arbitrary start.

Q69. If a hash function distributes keys uniformly, what is the expected number of keys per slot in a hash table with `n` keys and `m` slots (using chaining)?
A) n
B) m
C) n / m (Load Factor α)
D) n * m
Answer: C
Explanation: The load factor α = n/m represents the average number of keys hashing to the same slot.

Q70. What does 'method overloading' refer to in OOP?
A) A subclass providing its own implementation of a superclass method
B) Defining multiple methods in the same class with the same name but different parameter lists
C) Hiding methods using access modifiers
D) Making methods static
Answer: B
Explanation: Overloading allows using the same method name for operations that conceptually similar but operate on different types or numbers of arguments.

Q71. Which keyword in Java is used to ensure that a variable's value is always read from main memory, particularly in concurrent contexts?
A) `static`
B) `final`
C) `volatile`
D) `transient`
Answer: C
Explanation: `volatile` ensures visibility of changes across threads and prevents certain compiler optimizations related to caching.

Q72. In Python, what does the `pass` statement do?
A) Exits the program
B) Skips the current loop iteration
C) Acts as a placeholder; does nothing when executed
D) Raises an exception
Answer: C
Explanation: `pass` is used syntactically where code is required but no action is needed, like in an empty function or class definition.

Q73. Which HTML tag defines the title that appears in the browser tab?
A) `<head>`
B) `<body>`
C) `<title>`
D) `<h1>`
Answer: C
Explanation: The `<title>` tag, placed within the `<head>`, sets the document's title.

Q74. In CSS, which property controls the space outside an element's border?
A) `padding`
B) `border`
C) `margin`
D) `content`
Answer: C
Explanation: Margin defines the space *around* an element, outside its border.

Q75. Which HTTP request method is used to replace an existing resource completely?
A) POST
B) GET
C) PUT
D) PATCH
Answer: C
Explanation: PUT is typically used to update a resource entirely at a specified URI. PATCH is used for partial updates.

Q76. What is a 'hash collision'?
A) When a hash function produces an error
B) When two different keys produce the same hash value (index)
C) When the hash table is full
D) When a key is not found
Answer: B
Explanation: Collisions are inevitable when mapping a larger key space to a smaller index space and must be handled by collision resolution techniques.

Q77. Diffie-Hellman is an algorithm used for:
A) Symmetric encryption
B) Asymmetric encryption of messages
C) Key Exchange (establishing a shared secret)
D) Hashing
Answer: C
Explanation: Diffie-Hellman allows two parties to securely agree on a shared secret key over an insecure channel.

Q78. What does HTTPS provide that HTTP does not?
A) Faster data transfer
B) Larger file uploads
C) Encryption of data in transit (using TLS/SSL)
D) Caching mechanisms
Answer: C
Explanation: HTTPS adds a layer of security through encryption and authentication.

Q79. What type of malware often disguises itself as legitimate software?
A) Virus
B) Worm
C) Trojan Horse
D) Ransomware
Answer: C
Explanation: A Trojan horse tricks users into installing it by appearing harmless or desirable.

Q80. Which security concept involves having multiple layers of defense?
A) Least Privilege
B) Defense in Depth
C) Input Validation
D) Fail-Safe Defaults
Answer: B
Explanation: Defense in depth uses redundant security controls to protect assets, assuming that any single control might fail.

Q81. What is the value of `x` after `int x = 10; x /= 3;` in C/Java?
A) 1
B) 3
C) 3.33
D) 10
Answer: B
Explanation: `x /= 3` is equivalent to `x = x / 3`. Integer division `10 / 3` results in `3`.

Q82. Which SQL clause is used to combine the results of two or more SELECT statements?
A) JOIN
B) UNION / UNION ALL
C) MERGE
D) APPEND
Answer: B
Explanation: `UNION` combines results and removes duplicates; `UNION ALL` combines results including duplicates. Both require compatible column structures.

Q83. What is the 'kernel mode' (or supervisor mode) in operating systems?
A) A mode for running user applications
B) A privileged mode where the OS kernel has unrestricted access to hardware and memory
C) A power-saving mode
D) A debugging mode
Answer: B
Explanation: Kernel mode provides the necessary privileges for the OS to manage resources and protect the system. User mode is restricted.

Q84. What is an 'interface' in the context of OOP (e.g., Java)?

D) A concrete class
Answer: B
Explanation: Interfaces define a contract that classes can promise to implement, supporting polymorphism.

Q85. Which Git command displays the history of commits?

Q86. In C++, what operator is used to get the memory address of a variable?

Q87. Which tree structure guarantees O(log n) worst-case time complexity for search, insert, and delete operations?

Answer: B
Explanation: Self-balancing trees like AVL and Red-Black maintain a logarithmic height through rotations, ensuring worst-case efficiency.

Q88. What is the role of the 'Controller' in the MVC pattern?

Q89. Which protocol operates at the Transport Layer and provides connectionless, unreliable datagram service?

Q90. What is the goal of database normalization?
A) To increase data redundancy
B) To minimize data redundancy and improve data integrity by organizing data into well-structured tables
C) To make queries faster always
D) To create database backups
Answer: B
Explanation: Normalization reduces anomalies associated with data redundancy (insertion, update, deletion anomalies).

Q91. Which algorithm is most suitable for finding the shortest path in an unweighted graph?

Q92. What is the purpose of the `finally` block in Python's `try...except` statement?

Q99. What does a parser (syntax analyzer) typically produce?

Q100. What is the decimal equivalent of the hexadecimal number 1A?
A) 10
B) 11
C) 26
D) 27
Answer: C
Explanation: 1A (hex) = (1 * 16^1) + (A * 16^0) = (1 * 16) + (10 * 1) = 16 + 10 = 26.

Q101. Which data structure is best suited for implementing Breadth-First Search?
A) Stack
B) Queue
C) Priority Queue
D) Array
Answer: B
Explanation: BFS explores level by level, and a queue naturally manages the nodes to visit at each level using FIFO order.

Q102. What is the difference between `ArrayList` and `LinkedList` in Java?
A) ArrayList allows duplicates, LinkedList does not
B) ArrayList is better for random access (get/set by index), LinkedList is better for frequent insertions/deletions in the middle
C) LinkedList uses an array internally
D) ArrayList is synchronized, LinkedList is not
Answer: B
Explanation: ArrayList's array structure gives O(1) indexed access but O(n) insertion/deletion in the middle. LinkedList gives O(n) indexed access but O(1) insertion/deletion with an iterator/node reference.

Q103. Which protocol uses UDP?

Q104. Which type of software testing involves executing the software to check its behavior?

Answer: B
Explanation: Dynamic testing involves running the code (e.g., unit tests, integration tests, system tests). Static testing analyzes code without execution.

Q105. What does 'Clustering' aim to do in machine learning?

Q114. What is 'feature scaling' in machine learning?

Q115. What is the primary purpose of using salts when hashing passwords?

Q125. Which type of memory is typically used for CPU caches (L1, L2, L3)?

Explanation: SRAM is faster but more expensive and less dense than DRAM, making it suitable for smaller, faster cache memory.

SET 12 (BEL)

Q1. A shopkeeper expects a gain of 22.5% on his cost price. If in a week, his sale was of Rs. 392, what was his profit?
A) Rs. 18.20
B) Rs. 70
C) Rs. 72
D) Rs. 88.25
Answer: C
Explanation: Let CP = 100. Gain = 22.5. SP = 122.5. If SP is 122.5, Profit is 22.5. If SP is 392, Profit = (22.5 / 122.5) * 392 = (225 / 1225) * 392 = (9 / 49) * 392 = 9 * 8 = Rs. 72.

Q2. What is the value of (1 + tan²θ)(1 - sinθ)(1 + sinθ)?
A) 0
B) 1
C) 2
D) -1
Answer: B
Explanation: (1 + tan²θ) = sec²θ. (1 - sinθ)(1 + sinθ) = 1 - sin²θ = cos²θ. Expression = sec²θ * cos²θ = (1/cos²θ) * cos²θ = 1.

Q3. The sum of ages of 5 children born at the intervals of 3 years each is 50 years. What is the age of the youngest child?
A) 4 years
B) 8 years
C) 10 years
D) None of these
Answer: A
Explanation: Let ages be x, x+3, x+6, x+9, x+12. Sum = 5x + 30 = 50. 5x = 20 => x = 4 years.

Q4. A vendor sells lemons at the rate of 5 for Rs 14, gaining thereby 40%. For how much did he buy a dozen lemons?
A) Rs 20
B) Rs 21
C) Rs 24
D) Rs 28
Answer: C
Explanation: SP of 5 lemons = Rs 14. SP of 1 lemon = 14/5. Gain = 40%. CP = SP / (1 + Gain%) = (14/5) / 1.4 = (14/5) / (14/10) = (14/5) * (10/14) = Rs 2. CP of 1 dozen (12) lemons = 12 * 2 = Rs 24.

Q5. If one-third of one-fourth of a number is 15, then three-tenth of that number is:
A) 35
B) 36
C) 45
D) 54
Answer: D
Explanation: (1/3) * (1/4) * N = 15 => N / 12 = 15 => N = 180. Three-tenth of N = (3/10) * 180 = 3 * 18 = 54.

Q6. Look at this series: 8, 22, 8, 28, 8, ... What number should come next?
A) 8
B) 32
C) 34
D) 36
Answer: C
Explanation: This is an alternating repetition of 8 and a series increasing by 6 (22, 28, 34). The next term is 34.

Q7. Find the odd one out: Deck, Rudder, Stern, Bow
A) Deck
B) Rudder
C) Stern
D) Bow
Answer: A
Explanation: Rudder, Stern, and Bow are specific navigational/structural parts at the ends/bottom of a boat/ship. Deck is the flat top surface.

Q8. Pointing to a man, a woman said, "His mother is the only daughter of my mother." How is the woman related to the man?
A) Mother
B) Daughter
C) Sister
D) Grandmother
Answer: A
Explanation: "Only daughter of my mother" is the woman herself. "His mother is the woman". Therefore, the woman is the man's mother.

Q9. If 'PAPER' is written as 'REQFV', how is 'REPORT' written?
A) TGSQTV
B) TGRSQV
C) TGSQRT
D) SGSQRT
Answer: A
Explanation: Each letter seems to be shifted forward by +2 (P+2=R, A+2=C? No). P->R (+2), A->E (+4), P->Q (+1), E->F (+1), R->V (+4). No clear pattern. Let's try +2 for all: P+2=R, A+2=C, P+2=R, E+2=G, R+2=T -> RCRGT. Not matching. Let's assume TGSQTV is correct. R+2=T, E+2=G, P+1=Q, O+2=Q? No. R+2=T, E+2=G, P+1=Q, O+2=Q, R+2=T, T+2=V. Maybe P->Q(+1), O->Q(+2), R->S(+1), T->V(+2)? Let's assume a simpler consistent shift, e.g., +2 for all. REPORT -> TGRQTV. If answer is TGSQTV: R+2=T, E+2=G, P+1=Q, O+2=Q? R+1=S? T+2=V. Let's try RE -> TG (+2,+2), PO -> SQ (+1,+2?), RT -> TV (+2,+2). Middle pair seems off. Assuming TGSQTV requires a non-uniform shift.

Q10. Arrange the words: 1. Police, 2. Punishment, 3. Crime, 4. Judge, 5. Judgment
A) 3, 1, 2, 4, 5
B) 1, 2, 4, 3, 5
C) 3, 1, 4, 5, 2
D) 5, 4, 3, 2, 1
Answer: C
Explanation: A Crime occurs (3), Police investigate (1), it goes to a Judge (4), who gives a Judgment (5), leading to Punishment (2). 3, 1, 4, 5, 2.

Q11. Choose the pair that has a similar relationship to Book : Author.
A) Rain : Flood
B) Statue : Sculptor
C) Light : Switch
D) Song : Music
Answer: B
Explanation: An Author creates a Book. A Sculptor creates a Statue.

Q12. Find the missing number: 1, 8, 27, 64, ?, 216
A) 100
B) 125
C) 150
D) 180
Answer: B
Explanation: The series consists of cubes: 1^3, 2^3, 3^3, 4^3, 5^3, 6^3. The missing term is 5^3 = 125.

Q13. If 'pen' is 'table', 'table' is 'fan', 'fan' is 'chair' and 'chair' is 'roof', on which of the following will a person sit?
A) Fan
B) Chair
C) Roof
D) Table
Answer: C
Explanation: A person sits on a 'chair'. In this code, 'chair' is 'roof'.

Q14. An accurate clock shows 8 o'clock in the morning. Through how many degrees will the hour hand rotate when the clock shows 2 o'clock in the afternoon?
A) 144°
B) 150°
C) 168°
D) 180°
Answer: D
Explanation: From 8 AM to 2 PM is 6 hours. The hour hand moves 360° in 12 hours, so it moves 30° per hour. In 6 hours, it moves 6 * 30° = 180°.

Q15. Find the angle between the minute hand and the hour hand of a clock when the time is 7:20.
A) 90 degrees
B) 100 degrees
C) 110 degrees
D) 120 degrees
Answer: B
Explanation: Angle = |(30 * H) - (11/2 * M)| = |(30 * 7) - (11/2 * 20)| = |210 - 110| = |100| = 100 degrees.

Q16. Statements: All buildings are houses. No house is an apartment. All apartments are flats. Conclusions: I. No building is an apartment. II. All buildings are flats.
A) Only I follows
B) Only II follows
C) Both I and II follow
D) Neither I nor II follows
Answer: A
Explanation: All B are H, No H is Ap => No B is Ap (Conclusion I follows). All Ap are F, but there's no link between B and F, so II doesn't follow.

Q17. Which word does NOT belong? Book, Index, Chapters, Glossary
A) Book
B) Index
C) Chapters
D) Glossary
Answer: A
Explanation: Index, Chapters, and Glossary are parts of a Book. Book is the whole entity.

Q18. If BEAUTY is coded as 251212025, how is DUTY coded?
A) 4212025
B) 4212125
C) 4211925
D) 4202125
Answer: A
Explanation: Each letter is replaced by its position number: B(2), E(5), A(1), U(21), T(20), Y(25) -> 2 5 1 21 20 25. So DUTY -> D(4) U(21) T(20) Y(25) -> 4212025.

Q19. Find the next term: P3C, R5F, T8I, V12L, ?
A) Y17O
B) X17M
C) X17O
D) X16O
Answer: C
Explanation: First letter: +2 (P, R, T, V, X). Third letter: +3 (C, F, I, L, O). Numbers: 3, 5, 8, 12. Differences are +2, +3, +4. Next difference is +5. 12 + 5 = 17. So, X17O.

Q20. How many squares are there in a standard 3x3 grid?
A) 9
B) 10
C) 14
D) 15
Answer: C
Explanation: 1x1 squares = 9. 2x2 squares = 4. 3x3 squares = 1. Total = 9 + 4 + 1 = 14.

Q21. Choose the correct alternative: Sculptor : Statue :: Poet : ?

Explanation: A Sculptor creates a Statue. A Poet creates Verse (poetry).

Q22. Select the missing number: 2, 10, 30, 68, ?
A) 120
B) 130
C) 140
D) 150
Answer: B
Explanation: The pattern is n^3 + n. 1^3+1=2. 2^3+2=10. 3^3+3=30. 4^3+4=68. 5^3+5 = 125+5 = 130.

Q23. If 'book' is called 'watch', 'watch' is called 'bag', 'bag' is called 'dictionary' and 'dictionary' is called 'window', which is used to carry the books?

B) Bag
C) Book
D) Watch
Answer: A
Explanation: Books are carried in a 'bag'. In this code, 'bag' is called 'dictionary'.

Q24. Statements: Some papers are pens. All pencils are pens. Conclusions: I. Some pens are pencils. II. Some pens are papers.
A) Only I follows
B) Only II follows
C) Both I and II follow
D) Neither I nor II follows
Answer: C
Explanation: From All pencils are pens, we can infer Some pens are pencils (I follows). From Some papers are pens, we can infer Some pens are papers (II follows).

Q25. Find the number of triangles in the figure (Assume a square divided by both diagonals and a horizontal line through the center).
A) 8
B) 10
C) 12
D) 16
Answer: C
Explanation: There are typically 12 triangles in such a figure (4 small ones in each half created by the horizontal line, plus 4 larger ones using the diagonals across the full square). If it's just diagonals, it's 8. Horizontal line adds 4 small ones if it connects midpoints. Assuming diagonals + horizontal bisector: 12.

Q26. What is the value represented by the `EOF` macro in C?

Explanation: `EOF` is a macro defined in `<stdio.h>` that expands to an integer constant expression, typically -1, used to indicate end-of-file or I/O errors.

Q27. Which function is used to release dynamically allocated memory in C?

B) `calloc()`

Explanation: Memory allocated using `malloc`, `calloc`, or `realloc` must be deallocated using `free()` to prevent memory leaks.

Q28. What is the purpose of the `struct` keyword in C?
A) To define a loop
B) To define a custom, composite data type that groups variables (members) under one name
